< text>
This is my favorite fresh, organic, local restaurant. The food is amazingly delicious. Not only do they have the best Pho üç≤ I have ever tasted, they do tasty curries and more. I love combining fresh coconut juice straight from the coconut with my meals and it‚Äôs a naturally sweat and healthy option for the kids üëç.

The owner, Quinn ( I call her The Mighty Quinn üòâ ) checks in with her customers to make sure they are satisfied with their meals and enjoyed the Qochon experience.

I do miss visiting the restaurant during the SIP and am grateful they are able to continue to stay open and serve the community.

They are open for take out and delivery from Monday- Friday 11am - 5pm. They have a simple online order platform at QOCHON.COM. They offer free delivery to all orders over $25 and are located within a 10 miles radius.

Currently, they are running a campaign called GIFT-A-MEAL. Customers can purchase egift cards for meal donations to local frontline workers. Or you can donate directly on their website. Every $500 we raise equates to 50 meals. There is no minimum for donations so anyone can gift any amount you are comfortable with.

I highly recommend Qochon!<//text>

I was recommended this place by a friend and I loved it! Honestly, there aren't many breakfast places in Irvine that I like but the proved to be a new favorite. < text>
Board House Coffee is a new, independent Coffee Shop that serves up great coffee.

My cup of single origin Papua New Guinea had a strong, bold and rich flavor.  The quality was the best and the $1 refill made it a great value.

For breakfast, I had the bagel cream cheese lox(includes cucumber, capers, dill).  This was the best I've had in WLA.

I was very hungry, so I also had their California Club sandwich with turkey, ham, bacon, cheddar, swiss on a pretzel roll...another winner and enough food for lunch later as well.

My Maple Scone dessert had just the right flavor-not too sweet with a delicious buttery accent.

The atmosphere is great for study, meetings and also quick takeouts with parking(cafe is in Vinci Plaza).

The team of Steve and Andrew did an outstanding job being courteous and prompt with orders.

Verdict:  Board House Coffee  is my #1 choice for coffee, scones and sandwiches in WLA.

Surf's Up!<//text>

<Text>Eureka Restaurant & Lounge has remained a beacon for all of us looking for a place to park our cushy posteriors, escape the doldrums (or hurricanes) of everyday life and just enjoy cocktails and food served by the friendliest staff in an atmosphere that is welcoming, warm, tasteful, relaxing, unpretentious and cozy! It's like Cheers, where everyone knows your name...but throw in a rainbow unicorn. :)

Over the past few years, I've visited Eureka numerous times with family, friends, co-workers and blind dates (guilty as charged) for occasions ranging from birthdays to engagements to happy hours to work meetings to venting sessions to break ups (again...guilty as charged). And every time, the food, the service, the staff and the atmosphere has been consistently FAHbulous!

Whether its their inventive cocktail menu (Vesper anyone?) or their delicious food menu (Fried Chicken, Chicken Livers, Okra, Pot Roast, Deviled Eggs, Steak and just this week Shrimp and Grits!!!) or their wonderful and extremely hard-working service staff, they hit it out of the ballpark each and every time.

My husband (yes, why thank you!) and I go to Eureka for date night every Friday and we both look forward not only to the food and drinks, the friendly staff, the owners who are always around to greet you, the AHmazing atmosphere that permeates even my jaded heart and makes me smile, the smiles and laughs from all the diners as they catch up on each others lives and friends old and new meet, but also the sense of being in a place that is warm and welcoming and a respite from the harsh and cold world...well, foggy and windy since this IS San Francisco. There is nothing to beat that feeling!

And you can see the hard work put in by the staff, whether its managing the 530PM happy hour rush hour making sure every guest is looked after or chatting up customers asking how they are doing or asking if they want another round of cocktails or balancing 6 cocktails AND walking up the stairs with a smile on their face or just being around in case you need anything...you can see the passion, drive and hard work on their faces and its evident that Eureka is a mainstay in the Castro and its a place that truly feels wonderful every time I go there and I look forward to many, many more such wonderful times.

To the staff at Eureka...pom-poms off to ya! Keep up the good work and thank you for providing this wonderful place!< /Text><Pictures>None< /Pictures>< gmapID>

< rating>
5<//rating>
< Review>
Ambience - Quite nice. Good place to chill.
Fried Chicken - Quite good. Very generous portion.
Grilled Salmon - Great. Good portion served with mashed potato and vegetable. Personally I liked it more than fried chicken.
Service staff - very friendly and pleasant. Best service I experienced during my visit to San Fran!
My friends enjoyed their steak too!

I was there a few days ago with my friends (a group of 8) while visiting castro street in San Francisco. Their service staff set a table for us at the upper floor, their bar & lounge. The ambience was nice and definitely felt like a good place to chill. They even brought lit candles to our table!!!

Shorlty after we placed our order, ice water, bread and butter were served before our ordered food came. Being asians, we usually dont like bread that much but we tried theirs and we loved it. And the waiting staff very thoughtfully brought us another serving of bread after seeing how much we enjoyed it! Two thumbs up!!!! And they let my friend try their wine first before she ordered one and she enjoyed her wine too.

Our food came soon enough and as I said ealier, we all enjoyed their food and service.

Overall, a great experience and the best service among a few restaurants we went during our short visit to LA, Vegas and San Fransisco.

P.S. I dont usually write reviews. In fact, this is my first time writing a review here. Their service was so good that I had to write one. :)< /Review>

< text>
Was terrific in the past, clever, chill, upscale.  It was a great place for locals and to bring out of town friends.  Now it's effectively become the taco shop dining room and reeeeks of greasy food. The pile of paper plates in the trash bin at the entrance to the bar makes for a interesting, if not unpleasant welcome.  I had to bus a spot and get rid of the paper boats to have a place for our group to sit.  Be careful of the short stools.  They're all so wobbly, shopworn, and pooly maintained that you might just end up on the floor.  The stools seems to reveal what the place has become.   But, it's still got potential.  A little attention to some details and it could be great.  The drinks were good. That's a good place to start.  It is what it is.<//text>

< Rate>

<text>Most of the cocktails are pretty amazing, tho I had one I didn't think was all that great.  They are also priced very reasonably for top of the line product.  The entry procedure is fun, and not too well hidden.  The decor is very well done and fun. The only small quibbles I have are not having an integrated way to pay for food from the restaurant in front while having a card held in back for a bar tab, and seating/places to set food plates could be a bit better.  Those are pretty minor quibbles tho.

All in all a pretty cool place, and very good for b-day celebration..</text>< Pics>

< review>
This location is stunning! Floor to ceiling windows, lively atmosphere, cute decor, and great branding. The service was on point and very friendly. It‚Äôs been a long time since I had a server tell me their name and offer to tell me about the menu.

Menu consists of traditional and non traditional dishes. I would guess the most popular are the hummus bowls which are a bowl of hummus with toppings. Overall the food was ok. I would say pretty typical but served in a more trendy way. The pita bread was unique. Quite a bit more puffy then normal. It would be nice if the pita was fresh (crispy outside, and soft inside), instead of just kept in a warmer tray all day.

They have a take out section that didn‚Äôt have anyone working. The rest of the restaurant is all sit down. Not the typical order at the counter Mediterranean fare. I‚Äôll be back to try again and enjoy the great atmosphere.<//review>

< Text>
Oren's Hummus is a fairly new addition to the Cupertino Main Street shopping plaza, and it is definitely a welcome sight. There are plenty of Chinese dining options in the area due to the city it's located in, but Oren's provides a depth to the dining choices in this hip new plaza. My must orders are; Hummus Sabich (great fried eggplant with creamy Hummus all wrapped in a warm and fluffy pita bread), chicken rice bowl (the rice has great flavors and the chicken is tender with great spices), beef kebab (great spices again and it comes with two dips or sides), and sweet potato fries (comes out piping hot with red pepper mayo).
After chowing down on this big meal, I walked out feeling healthy and not weighed down with all the grease found in other restaurants. Oren's provide a fresh alternative to eat healthy while enjoying good ingredients prepared well. I would definitely return to enjoy another "healthy-decision" meal.<//Text>

< user_name>
Irina Kim</user_name>
< text>
I work nearby so I come here every once in a while to grab the Chicken Schnitzel - great, crispy chicken at a moderate price. I'm sure there are cheaper hummus places near here, and Oren's is one of many in the immediate area competing for the same Mediterranean niche (TKS, Falafel Stop, House of Falafel, etc.) but Oren's has some interesting spins on classic dishes.

I'm a sucker for their coleslaw with how cilantro-heavy and vinegar-y it is - probably a hit or miss for most people.</text>
